\hypertarget{namespacescifir}{}\doxysection{scifir Namespace Reference}
\label{namespacescifir}\index{scifir@{scifir}}


The namespace scifir contains all scifir-\/units, excepting the string literals, which are outside.

class \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1dimension}{dimension}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Class that represents dimensions of the SI system of units. Each prefix sizes 6 bytes, 1 byte for the dimension type, 1 byte for the prefix, 1 byte for the position (which can be the NUMERATOR or the DENOMINATOR), and 3 bytes for the custom dimension (in case it\textquotesingle{}s used one). \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
class \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1prefix}{prefix}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Class that represents prefixes of the SI system of units. Each prefix sizes 1 byte. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
class \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1scalar__unit}{scalar\+\_\+unit}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Class that allows to create scalar units, which are cmoposed of a value (as a float) and dimensions. The dimensions can be of any number, and be basic dimensions and/or abbreviations of dimensions. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
class \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1vector__unit__2d}{vector\+\_\+unit\+\_\+2d}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Class that creates a vector unit in 2D. The vector is in {\bfseries{polar coordinates}} with a value and dimensions of the \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1scalar__unit}{scalar\+\_\+unit}}, and an angle theta for his direction. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
class \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1vector__unit__3d}{vector\+\_\+unit\+\_\+3d}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Class that creates a vector unit in 3D. The vector is in {\bfseries{spherical coordinates}} with a value and dimensions of the \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1scalar__unit}{scalar\+\_\+unit}}, and an angle theta and another angle phi for his direction. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
class \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1vector__unit__nd}{vector\+\_\+unit\+\_\+nd}}
\item 
struct \mbox{\hyperlink{structscifir_1_1is__number}{is\+\_\+number}}

\item

float \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacescifir_add12c2189775431391a01da44451c555}{asinh\+\_\+degree}} (float x)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Calculates the asinh receiving x in degrees. It uses the \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacescifir_ac003e3c2113237706f4c4c50164a4024}{asinh()}} function of the standard library of C++, but the difference is that the argument is in degrees, not in radians. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
float \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacescifir_aa30920e8c4e52f3c9f1087b97b053585}{acosh\+\_\+degree}} (float x)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Calculates the acosh receiving x in degrees. It uses the \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacescifir_a83266adde7a9639563d4ab6ae9090a7a}{acosh()}} function of the standard library of C++, but the difference is that the argument is in degrees, not in radians. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
float \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacescifir_a18598f24883d62e6686b822fd43451b8}{atanh\+\_\+degree}} (float x)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Calculates the atanh receiving x in degrees. It uses the \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacescifir_acb80729ddcfa267023fefe9d39abac38}{atanh()}} function of the standard library of C++, but the difference is that the argument is in degrees, not in radians. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
The namespace scifir contains all scifir-\/units, excepting the string literals, which are outside.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1angle}{angle}} scifir\+::angle\+\_\+between (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1vector__unit__nd}{vector\+\_\+unit\+\_\+nd}} \&}]{x,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1vector__unit__nd}{vector\+\_\+unit\+\_\+nd}} \&}]{y }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns the angle between two vectors x and y inside the ND space, which can be 2D or 3D, depending on the ND of the vectors. If the vectors have different ND, it returns an empty \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1vector__unit__nd}{vector\+\_\+unit\+\_\+nd}} instead.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1vector__unit__nd}{vector\+\_\+unit\+\_\+nd}} scifir\+::cross\+\_\+product (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1vector__unit__nd}{vector\+\_\+unit\+\_\+nd}} \&}]{x,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1vector__unit__nd}{vector\+\_\+unit\+\_\+nd}} \&}]{y }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates a \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1vector__unit__nd}{vector\+\_\+unit\+\_\+nd}} as the cross product of the two vectors x and y. If both vectors aren\textquotesingle{}t in 3D, it returns an empty \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1vector__unit__nd}{vector\+\_\+unit\+\_\+nd}}, because the cross product doesn\textquotesingle{}t exists outside 3D.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1dimension}{dimension}} $>$ scifir\+::divide\+\_\+dimensions (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1dimension}{dimension}} $>$}]{x,  }\item[{const vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1dimension}{dimension}} $>$ \&}]{y,  }\item[{long double \&}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Divides the first vector of dimensions with the other. The result is normalized after, which means that equal dimensions at the numerator and at the denominator are cancelled. It also updates the value associated with those two vectors of dimensions with the prefix m ath and the conversion factor of those dimensions.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{sin()}{sin()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily float scifir\+::sin (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classscifir_1_1angle}{angle}} \&}]{x }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Calculates the sin of angle x. It uses the \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacescifir_ad3b92cdb628eeec991c326c1727fdd9e}{sin()}} function of the standard library of C++, the difference is that angle is in degrees, not in radians.
